							<div id="siteNotice"><!-- CentralNotice --></div>
						<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en"><span dir="auto">List of bills in the 113th United States Congress</span></h1>
						<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-navigation">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><p>The <b>bills of the 113th United States Congress</b> list includes <a href="/wiki/Bill_(law)" title="Bill (law)">proposed federal laws</a> that were introduced in the <a href="/wiki/113th_United_States_Congress" title="113th United States Congress">113th United States Congress</a>. This Congress will last from January 3, 2013 to January 3, 2015.</p>
<p>The United States Congress is the <a href="/wiki/Bicameralism" title="Bicameralism">bicameral</a> <a href="/wiki/Legislature" title="Legislature">legislature</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Federal_government_of_the_United_States" title="Federal government of the United States">federal government</a> of the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> consisting of two houses: the lower house known as the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">House of Representatives</a> and the upper house known as the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">Senate</a>. The House and Senate are equal partners in the legislative process—legislation cannot be enacted without the consent of both chambers. The bills listed below are arranged on the basis of which chamber they were first introduced in, and then chronologically by date.</p>
<p>Once a bill is approved by one house, it is sent to the other which may pass, reject, or amend it. For the bill to become law, both houses must agree to identical versions of the bill. After passage by both houses, a bill is <a href="/wiki/Enrolled_bill" title="Enrolled bill">enrolled</a> and sent to the <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">president</a> for signature or <a href="/wiki/Veto" title="Veto">veto</a>. Bills from the 113th Congress that have successfully completed this process become public laws, listed as <a href="/wiki/Acts_of_the_113th_United_States_Congress" title="Acts of the 113th United States Congress">Acts of the 113th United States Congress</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<td><a href="/wiki/Bill_to_deny_visas_to_some_United_Nations_ambassadors_(S._2195;_113th_Congress)" title="Bill to deny visas to some United Nations ambassadors (S. 2195; 113th Congress)" class="mw-redirect">To deny admission to the United States to any representative to the United Nations</a> who has engaged in <a href="/wiki/Espionage" title="Espionage">espionage</a> activities against the United States, poses a threat to United States national security interests, or has engaged in a <a href="/wiki/Terrorist" title="Terrorist" class="mw-redirect">terrorist</a> activity against the United States.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://hdl.loc.gov/loc.uscongress/legislation.113s2199">S. 2199</a></td>
<td>April 1, 2014</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Paycheck_Fairness_Act_(S._2199;_113th_Congress)" title="Paycheck Fairness Act (S. 2199; 113th Congress)">Paycheck Fairness Act</a></td>
<td>A bill to amend the <a href="/wiki/Fair_Labor_Standards_Act_of_1938" title="Fair Labor Standards Act of 1938" class="mw-redirect">Fair Labor Standards Act of 1938</a> to provide more effective remedies to victims of discrimination in the payment of wages on the basis of sex, and for other purposes.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://hdl.loc.gov/loc.uscongress/legislation.113s2260">S. 2260</a></td>
<td>April 28, 2014</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/EXPIRE_Act_of_2014" title="EXPIRE Act of 2014" class="mw-redirect">EXPIRE Act of 2014</a></td>
<td>A bill to amend the <a href="/wiki/Internal_Revenue_Code_of_1986" title="Internal Revenue Code of 1986" class="mw-redirect">Internal Revenue Code of 1986</a> to extend certain expiring provisions, and for other purposes. (This bill is being amended on to the <a href="/wiki/Hire_More_Heroes_Act_of_2013_(H.R._3474;_113th_Congress)" title="Hire More Heroes Act of 2013 (H.R. 3474; 113th Congress)">Hire More Heroes Act of 2013 (H.R. 3474; 113th Congress)</a>. This process is called using a legislative vehicle.)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://hdl.loc.gov/loc.uscongress/legislation.113s2262">S. 2262</a></td>
<td>April 28, 2014</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Energy_Savings_and_Industrial_Competitiveness_Act_of_2014_(S._2262;_113th_Congress)" title="Energy Savings and Industrial Competitiveness Act of 2014 (S. 2262; 113th Congress)">Energy Savings and Industrial Competitiveness Act of 2014</a></td>
<td>A bill to promote energy savings in residential buildings and industry, and for other purposes.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://hdl.loc.gov/loc.uscongress/legislation.113s2270">S. 2270</a></td>
<td>April 29, 2014</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Insurance_Capital_Standards_Clarification_Act_of_2014_(S._2270;_113th_Congress)" title="Insurance Capital Standards Clarification Act of 2014 (S. 2270; 113th Congress)">Insurance Capital Standards Clarification Act of 2014</a></td>
<td>To clarify the application of certain leverage and risk-based requirements under the <a href="/wiki/Dodd-Frank_Wall_Street_Reform_and_Consumer_Protection_Act" title="Dodd-Frank Wall Street Reform and Consumer Protection Act" class="mw-redirect">Dodd-Frank Wall Street Reform and Consumer Protection Act</a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://hdl.loc.gov/loc.uscongress/legislation.113s2363">S. 2363</a></td>
<td>May 20, 2014</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Bipartisan_Sportsmen%27s_Act_of_2014_(S._2363;_113th_Congress)" title="Bipartisan Sportsmen's Act of 2014 (S. 2363; 113th Congress)">Bipartisan Sportsmen's Act of 2014</a></td>
<td>A bill to protect and enhance opportunities for recreational hunting, fishing, and shooting, and for other purposes.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://hdl.loc.gov/loc.uscongress/legislation.113s2569">S. 2569</a></td>
<td>July 8, 2014</td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Bring_Jobs_Home_Act_(S._2569;_113th_Congress)" title="Bring Jobs Home Act (S. 2569; 113th Congress)">Bring Jobs Home Act</a></td>
<td>A bill to provide an incentive for businesses to bring jobs back to America.</td>
</tr>
